  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_96f27cff-28ef-4dad-a1fa-edf4cc74880b'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText2252377549890660617" style="display:none"><b>Have you ever wondered what might have been?</b><br />Gemma Dawson is at the airport, staring at two plane tickets to two different cities. Two different weddings. Two possible futures. She’s at a crossroads.<br /><b>Be maid of honor at her best friend’s wedding or crash her ex’s?</b><br />Gemma’s decision, unknown to her, hinges on a delayed flight and a chance meeting. Now her life is about to go down two parallel tracks—will Gemma fly toward a life with her first love or a future with a man she’s not even met yet? <br /><br /><i>Love Connection</i> is a feel good Romantic Comedy about one woman, life’s infinite possibilities, and the destiny that lies beyond two different choices.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1773842532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9882728255676272324">(Source: I received a digital copy of this book for free on a read-to-review basis. Thanks to author Camilla Isley.)<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Jake.” I inhale deeply. “When I discovered you were getting married, my world collapsed.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This was an adult contemporary romance novel, following one woman as her life went in two different directions.<br/><br/>Gemma was an okay character, and it was clear how deep her feelings were for Jake. It was also nice how much she cared about her friend, that she’d sacrifice her own happi</span>
  <span id="freeText9882728255676272324" style="display:none">(Source: I received a digital copy of this book for free on a read-to-review basis. Thanks to author Camilla Isley.)<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Jake.” I inhale deeply. “When I discovered you were getting married, my world collapsed.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This was an adult contemporary romance novel, following one woman as her life went in two different directions.<br><br>Gemma was an okay character, and it was clear how deep her feelings were for Jake. It was also nice how much she cared about her friend, that she’d sacrifice her own happiness to help her.<br><br>The storyline in this followed Gemma as her life went down two different paths after one life-altering situation. In one life she went and stopped her ex’s wedding and told him how she felt, and in the other she went to her friend’s wedding instead. It was enjoyable to see these two different futures unfold, and I liked the mystery of who Gemma would end up with in the end, and whether the two futures would somehow merge.<br><br>The ending to this was pretty happy, and I was satisfied with the way things ended.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433081147i/15047180.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>6.5 out of 10</span>
  <a data-text-id="9882728255676272324" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1742097173" class="readable"
              >

  <span id="freeText6860872007784709924" style="display:none"><i>Love Connection</i> the perfect read for fans of <i>Sliding Doors...</i><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1495459682i/22818454._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt="chick lit series" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B01LXO39NU?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=camiisle-20&amp;camp=1789&amp;linkCode=xm2&amp;creativeASIN=B01LXO39NU" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a><br><a href="https://geo.itunes.apple.com/us/book/love-connection/id1319248867?mt=11&amp;at=1001ldac" rel="nofollow noopener">iBooks</a><br><a href="http://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/love-connection-camilla-isley/1124707490?ean=2940153753386" rel="nofollow noopener">Barned &amp; Noble</a><br><a href="https://play.google.com/store/books/details?id=y6kkDQAAQBAJ&amp;hl&amp;PAffiliateID=1011lLyJ" rel="nofollow noopener">Google Play</a><br><a href="http://www.kobobooks.com/search/search.html?q=1230001361223" rel="nofollow noopener">Kobo</a> <br><p><br>This is a romantic comedy about one woman, life’s infinite possibilities, and the destiny that lies beyond two opposite choices.</p></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3671295407244768557">This was an okay-novel.<br/><br/>The concept is unique, I can definitely give it that. Having two parallel-running story-lines with the same characters but different choices, intrigued me a lot at first. That is, until I noticed the author keep going back to the same things in both storylines.<br/>Although I do get the why, it got on my nerves she sometimes uses the exact same descriptions and dialogues in both story lines.<br/><br/>The other issue I had was conversations sometimes feeling very forced and the main chara</span>
  <span id="freeText3671295407244768557" style="display:none">This was an okay-novel.<br /><br />The concept is unique, I can definitely give it that. Having two parallel-running story-lines with the same characters but different choices, intrigued me a lot at first. That is, until I noticed the author keep going back to the same things in both storylines.<br />Although I do get the why, it got on my nerves she sometimes uses the exact same descriptions and dialogues in both story lines.<br /><br />The other issue I had was conversations sometimes feeling very forced and the main character having the tendency to have a childish whine-moment once in a while.<br /><br />It was a cute read, but it wasn't really anything special to me.<br /><br />3 / 5</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/32293825-love-connection">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44344367-elle-s-book-blog?shelf=chicklit">chicklit</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1800067299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13728809175372951080"><b> Release Date: </b> October 8, 2016<br/><b> Genre: </b> Chick Lit. Women's Fiction.<br/><br/><b> :: 5+ Pretty Little Stars :: </b><br/><br/>WOAH. This is one of the most <u> unique </u> books that I have read in a <u> long </u> time. Camilla Isley has outdone herself with this novel and I couldn't be more pleased with how it all turned out. What do you do when you have to make a decision? This is the essential plot of this book. One woman. Two life choices. Each with different endings. So what would she choose, and what happens when she gets there?<br/><br/>Thi</span>
  <span id="freeText13728809175372951080" style="display:none"><b> Release Date: </b> October 8, 2016<br /><b> Genre: </b> Chick Lit. Women's Fiction.<br /><br /><b> :: 5+ Pretty Little Stars :: </b><br /><br />WOAH. This is one of the most <u> unique </u> books that I have read in a <u> long </u> time. Camilla Isley has outdone herself with this novel and I couldn't be more pleased with how it all turned out. What do you do when you have to make a decision? This is the essential plot of this book. One woman. Two life choices. Each with different endings. So what would she choose, and what happens when she gets there?<br /><br />This book is AMAZING. I was a bit concerned at first thinking that the plot would be confusing as every other chapter features one of the life choices, and the next chapter the other. But this was NOT confusing at all. Perhaps its because it is so well written that we can easily follow along, or maybe its because we need to ALSO CHOOSE which path would be better suited. Either way, it's not a confusing story, rather one that is so interesting that you will be hooked. <br /><br />Anyway, I have now read a few of Camilla Isley's novels and I have to say that each and every time I have been impressed. Now I can't wait to see what the second book in the series is like... I am so excited! ~ Highly recommended!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13728809175372951080" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1766373570" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1766373570" />
    <a title="Amy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14045562-amy"><img alt="Amy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1542231656p2/14045562.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1766373570?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy" href="/user/show/14045562-amy">Amy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/31699007-love-connection">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14045562-amy?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1766373570" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13878145568822018854">Full review on <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.novelgossip.com'>www.novelgossip.com</a><br/><br/>This book caught my attention as I think we’ve all wondered how our lives could have turned out completely differently had we made other choices and in Love Connection you get to see how Gemma’s life could be by making both choices and seeing her two very unalike lives side by side. She can either attend her best friends wedding as the maid of honor, or crash her exes wedding and reveal her true feelings. Which choice does she really make? And will the outcome r</span>
  <span id="freeText13878145568822018854" style="display:none">Full review on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.novelgossip.com">www.novelgossip.com</a><br /><br />This book caught my attention as I think we’ve all wondered how our lives could have turned out completely differently had we made other choices and in Love Connection you get to see how Gemma’s life could be by making both choices and seeing her two very unalike lives side by side. She can either attend her best friends wedding as the maid of honor, or crash her exes wedding and reveal her true feelings. Which choice does she really make? And will the outcome really change much or is fate guiding her to the same place either way?<br /><br />Gemma is such a fun character. In fact, all of the characters here are loads of fun. Besides Gemma you have her best friend Amelia. The two are quite the pair and they have a deep friendship full of humor and true understanding. Several of their scenes made me giggle and after finishing such a heavy novel a bit of lighthearted fun was exactly what I needed. Jake is Gemma’s ex and the one that got away. He’s moved on and is getting married on the same day as Amelia, hence Gemma’s huge decision. Lastly there is Richard who is the new man in Gemma’s life. He is utterly charming and quite the catch but Gemma can’t quite seem to completely let go of her past and embrace her future.<br /><br />It was really fun and interesting to read this one. Every chapter alternates between both choices; one chapter with Gemma heading to Amelia’s wedding and the other to Jake’s. I was dying to see how it would all end and I was not disappointed, although I’m rather eager for book two in the series now! Filled with witty banter, humor and heart Love Connection is a delightful read that will make you feel good and leave you with a smile on your face. In fact, I smiled most of the way through this book and still am!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13878145568822018854" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2001467335" />
    <a title="Camilla Isley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32921088-camilla-isley"><img alt="Camilla Isley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1444931510p2/32921088.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2001467335?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Camilla Isley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Camilla Isley" href="/user/show/32921088-camilla-isley">Camilla Isley</a>
      </span>

          added it


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32921088-camilla-isley?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32921088-camilla-isley?shelf=stuff-i-wrote">stuff-i-wrote</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2001467335" class="readable"

    <a title="Debby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56322436-debby"><img alt="Debby" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598643499p2/56322436.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2469096693?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debby" href="/user/show/56322436-debby">Debby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56322436-debby?shelf=authors-i-j">authors-i-j</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2469096693" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6975170192266699690">(Audiobook Review)<br/><br/> I received Love Connection in a giveaway and found it to be a fun romantic comedy that makes you wonder about the choices you would make to find happiness. <br/><br/>The story deals with Gemma Dawson, who is an attorney from London. She sits at a Chicago airport bar, holding two tickets while contemplating if she should fly to her best friend’s wedding as the maid of honor or crash her ex-boyfriend’s wedding in California. After a few drinks, she eavesdrops on another heartbroken woman </span>
  <span id="freeText6975170192266699690" style="display:none">(Audiobook Review)<br /><br /> I received Love Connection in a giveaway and found it to be a fun romantic comedy that makes you wonder about the choices you would make to find happiness. <br /><br />The story deals with Gemma Dawson, who is an attorney from London. She sits at a Chicago airport bar, holding two tickets while contemplating if she should fly to her best friend’s wedding as the maid of honor or crash her ex-boyfriend’s wedding in California. After a few drinks, she eavesdrops on another heartbroken woman who happens to be a flight attendant. She discovers that her best friend’s fiancé has been carrying affair with this woman for over a year. The other alternative is that she’s never forgotten Jake, the love of her life and soulmate and needs to confess all to him before it’s too late. Thus begins the “What If” and the vignettes on each path that she chooses to get to her HEA.<br /><br />The audiobook of Love Connection by Camilla Isley flowed nicely into a well-written romance that had very entertaining characters, comical moments and serious dialogues between Gemma and those around her. It was light-hearted and a bit of a short novella on the “What If”. <br />The only drawback to this listen was the narration. I did not feel that the choice of narrator suited this story. The voice was a bit dry and did not punctuate the exclamatory parts in the story…i.e., parts that should have made you feel excitement or anger were not accentuated when needed.<br />I was thankful for receiving this audiobook giveaway and I look forward to listening dependent on narration or reading more form Ms. Isley. My rating would have been higher if not for the narration.<br /><br />4-Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="6975170192266699690" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2446102730" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2446102730" />
    <a title="Kay&#39;s Blushing Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74978311-kay-s-blushing-book-reviews"><img alt="Kay&#39;s Blushing Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521768118p2/74978311.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2446102730?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kay&#39;s Blushing Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kay&#39;s Blushing Book Reviews" href="/user/show/74978311-kay-s-blushing-book-reviews">Kay&#39;s Blushing Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/74978311-kay-s-blushing-book-reviews?shelf=rom-com">rom-com</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2446102730" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13832609899438895987"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1527751824i/25625053._SX540_.jpg' width='600' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Love Connection by Camilla Isley </i>
</b> <br/><br/><b>GENRE: Romance Comedy <br/>NARRATION: First Person (heroine)<br/>BOOK DETAILS: Standalone but book #1 of a connecting series First Comes Love <br/> AUDIO AVAILABLE? Yes - Whispersync for Voice-enabled </b><br/><br/><b> THE STORY:</b> <br/>Have you ever been at crossroads and not known which direction your meant to take?<br/>Your choice being so crucial it will literally be life changing? <br/>Have you ever wondered how your life would have turned out if you chose the other direction? Would the outcome inevit</span>
  <span id="freeText13832609899438895987" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1527751824i/25625053._SX540_.jpg" width="600" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Love Connection by Camilla Isley </i>
</b> <br><br><b>GENRE: Romance Comedy <br>NARRATION: First Person (heroine)<br>BOOK DETAILS: Standalone but book #1 of a connecting series First Comes Love <br> AUDIO AVAILABLE? Yes - Whispersync for Voice-enabled </b><br><br><b> THE STORY:</b> <br>Have you ever been at crossroads and not known which direction your meant to take?<br>Your choice being so crucial it will literally be life changing? <br>Have you ever wondered how your life would have turned out if you chose the other direction? Would the outcome inevitably be the same no matter your path? Believing your destiny has already been written and fate will guide you back to where you belong?<br><br>This is a story very cleverly and well written in a sliding doors scenario, following two parallel stories of Gemma Dawson and her journey back to her true love and happily ever after.<br><br><b>
  <i> One woman, two choices, two separate journeys, one destined ending.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1530791773i/25926946._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>MY THOUGHTS: </b><br>This story evokes some pretty relatable emotions for its readers. Doubt, indecisions, regret and questions. The writer grabbed my attention within the first few pages and I was completely engaged throughout the entire story. The good use of witty humour lightened the sadness throughout the story. You would think that all the back and forth between the two separate journeys would create some confusion, but Camilla’s talented writing ability created a smooth flowing and easy to follow story. <br><br>I have to mention that this is a very G rated romance. I needed more along the M rated romance though to feel their chemistry, passion and pain on a deeper level. Adding some intimacy or sweet bedroom moments would have helped connect the character’s motives to their emotions, therefore enhancing the intensity of their love for one another, making it more realistic.<br><br>Jake came across as a little detached and lacking in character depth for me because his presence wasn’t strong enough throughout the story. Yes, he is kind and sweet and easy going but who is he really? Not enough of his personality shone through for me to attach myself to him.<br><br>Overall,This was a really enjoyable and engaging story about friendship, the significance and consequences of our choices, true love and undeniable destiny.<br><br><b>I received an audio copy of this book in exchange for my honest review.</b><br> <br><b>MY RATINGS:</b> (All ratings are out of 5)<br>BLUSH RATING: 0<br>ROMANCE RATING:4<br>PLOT RATING: 5<br>OVERALL: 4 Blushing Stars <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1526032963i/25521738._SX540_.jpg" width="600" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Narrated by: Audra Cook<br> Length: 6h 11m<br><br>Initially I was completely thrown off by the robotic tone of the narrator, but after a while I adjusted and the audio flowed a little easier. Overall the dialogue parts for Gemma and Amelia were fine, but her narration of a male voice and narrative sections were off putting.<br><br>There were external sounds added (popping popcorn and cat purrs and meows) which I didn’t feel were necessary, and to be honest sounded weird.<br><br>Unfortunately, Audra’s voice just didn’t work for me, which is a shame because I really enjoyed the story.<br><br>AUDIO RATING: 3/5<br><br><b> <i> Liked my review? Follow my Blog or join me on Facebook for more reviews, Giveaways, Freebies and new release updates</i></b><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/kaysblushingbookreviews/">https://www.facebook.com/kaysblushing...</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://wordpress.com/media/kaysblushingbookreview.wordpress.com">https://wordpress.com/media/kaysblush...</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13832609899438895987" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1772829326" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1772829326" />
    <a title="Kristin  Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30889046-kristin-reads"><img alt="Kristin  Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546828523p2/30889046.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1772829326?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin  Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin  Reads" href="/user/show/30889046-kristin-reads">Kristin  Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/32293825-love-connection">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1772829326" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14451556560244634191">I absolutely loved this book. What I love most about Camilla Isley, is that she has this ability to not only write a story you can not put down. But she is able to add the romance , the comedy , and the drama is a "clean" way. <br/> <br/>This book has so many great elements. One of those elements is the dynamic between two BFF Amelia and Gemma. They really are my favorite. The way these two stand by each other, love each other and is there through good and bad is AMAZING. It is one of my favorite BFF duos</span>
  <span id="freeText14451556560244634191" style="display:none">I absolutely loved this book. What I love most about Camilla Isley, is that she has this ability to not only write a story you can not put down. But she is able to add the romance , the comedy , and the drama is a "clean" way. <br /> <br />This book has so many great elements. One of those elements is the dynamic between two BFF Amelia and Gemma. They really are my favorite. The way these two stand by each other, love each other and is there through good and bad is AMAZING. It is one of my favorite BFF duos I have ever read! They are hilarious despite what is going on. I know y'all will just adore them.<br /><br />There are also three men you will fall in love with. Dylan, Jake and Robert. Even though the story maybe different for all three of these guy. I certainly loved being apart of their story. Like I said before this book is full of surprise elements and twist and turns, that give a good dose of what ifs and fate that will make your heart full! This is a #mustread<br /></span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2215879288" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14641175948033331450">Cute book and interesting concept with the whole "how would one choice affect your life?" The characters were rather one-dimensional though, and I kind of wish that it didn't have the whole "soul mates" theme going on with the ending being the same for either choice. I mean, I get the "it was meant to be" thing, but it just puts a damper to the fact that the choice was supposed to alter her life, since it's basically saying that not much would have changed after all.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68294182-jules-bookverse?shelf=review">review</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2044083639" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18212636700745752999">Ok guys, I just finished this book and am sorting through amazing emotions like joy. There's sadness, happiness, laughing and crying at the same time.<br/><br/>I was intrigued starting at chapter 2 when I realized that you see both option she could choose. I felt embarrassed with Gemma as she had to cancel a wedding, looking like hell, after riding on a hay/chicken transporter. Laughed my ass off at her inner conversations with herself and had a hard time to decide which way would be my choice. Once I lik</span>
  <span id="freeText18212636700745752999" style="display:none">Ok guys, I just finished this book and am sorting through amazing emotions like joy. There's sadness, happiness, laughing and crying at the same time.<br /><br />I was intrigued starting at chapter 2 when I realized that you see both option she could choose. I felt embarrassed with Gemma as she had to cancel a wedding, looking like hell, after riding on a hay/chicken transporter. Laughed my ass off at her inner conversations with herself and had a hard time to decide which way would be my choice. Once I liked one option better and loved the new characters introduced the other path came running back with some golden points in his pocket, like a mother-in-law who just rocks! <br /><br />I loved that there were a lot of movie examples, for certain situation. It just gave you the perfect idea for that scene and was hilarious as hell. Just saying Sex-and-the-city and 27-Dresses vibes going on here! ;)<br /><br />Getting closer to the end it even got a bit mysterious because of a special bachelorette/hen party activity. By then I was wondering if Gemma would be dreaming or even living both lives. :D <br /><br />The ending just took my breath away and I finally could decide what's best for all. Crying over how cute and romantic the two worlds are combined I can just recommend this book to all romantic birds out there who love not only to cry but to laugh full of joy!!<br /><br />All in all I really liked this book and am so glad I got to read it. Thanks at the author and goodreads again for this amazing giveaway prize!! </span>

<div id="review_2450445401" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2450445401" />
    <a title="Effie Kammenou" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19371467-effie-kammenou"><img alt="Effie Kammenou" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438130201p2/19371467.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2450445401?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Effie Kammenou" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Effie Kammenou" href="/user/show/19371467-effie-kammenou">Effie Kammenou</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2450445401" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2827911407463588940">Have you ever been at a crossroad and wondered which path to take? Camilla Isley explores this dilemma in The Love Connection. It’s quite an interesting concept to write side by side stories in the same novel. <br/>Gemma, the main character, has two airline tickets in her possession – one will take her to her best friend’s wedding and the other to her ex-boyfriend’s wedding, a man she never stopped loving. In one story, she chooses to attend her friend’s wedding in order to stop her from marrying a p</span>
  <span id="freeText2827911407463588940" style="display:none">Have you ever been at a crossroad and wondered which path to take? Camilla Isley explores this dilemma in The Love Connection. It’s quite an interesting concept to write side by side stories in the same novel. <br />Gemma, the main character, has two airline tickets in her possession – one will take her to her best friend’s wedding and the other to her ex-boyfriend’s wedding, a man she never stopped loving. In one story, she chooses to attend her friend’s wedding in order to stop her from marrying a philandering man. In the other story, she goes to stop the wedding of her old love and plead for him to choose her instead.<br />There are a lot of amusing moments and some of it you know could never happen in the real world. But that is what romantic comedies are for – to delve into a world of romantic fantasy and laugh over unlikely situations.<br />The Love Connection was more than a simple romance. I found myself wondering about the paths I’ve had to choose and where I would be if I had made different choices. Would fate and destiny intervene and land me where I am today? Or would my life be completely different? These questions will be answered by the end of the book.<br />I listened to the audio version of this book, narrated by Audra Cook. The narration was done very well. Ms. Cook spoke clearly and did a nice job varying the voices. Her execution was enjoyable and pleasant.<br />I would definitely read or listen to another book by this author.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2827911407463588940" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3016466244" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3016466244" />
    <a title="Bookworm" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31167656-bookworm"><img alt="Bookworm" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508209904p2/31167656.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3016466244?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bookworm" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bookworm" href="/user/show/31167656-bookworm">Bookworm</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3016466244" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6140144269327362823">This is the first of three stories by this author that I received an ARC through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review. I was in the mood for swoon-worthy chick lit and this seemed to fit the bill. The plot concept was intriguing. A woman has 2 plane tickets - one to her best friend’s wedding and another to her ex-boyfriend/soul mate’s wedding - and must choose which road to go down. Does she choose loyalty to her friend or does she crash her exe’s wedding to tell him her true feelings befo</span>
  <span id="freeText6140144269327362823" style="display:none">This is the first of three stories by this author that I received an ARC through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review. I was in the mood for swoon-worthy chick lit and this seemed to fit the bill. The plot concept was intriguing. A woman has 2 plane tickets - one to her best friend’s wedding and another to her ex-boyfriend/soul mate’s wedding - and must choose which road to go down. Does she choose loyalty to her friend or does she crash her exe’s wedding to tell him her true feelings before it’s too late? The story portrays both choices so we get to know what happens in each situation. What sounded like a wild ride was actually mundane and dull. This story had tons of potential! But where things went off the rails for me was the lack of a plot arc in one of the scenarios, which made it uneventful; too much dialogue, which detracted from the emotional depth aspect; and no clear antagonist, which meant there was very little internal/external conflict and no character growth/transformation. The end message was too simple. There are many 4 and 5 star reviews for this book so there is clearly a niche. I think readers who enjoy light cozy romance books will get more from this than I did. I need more emotional depth in my women’s fiction.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6140144269327362823" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5883901602903885485">Stormi originally read this for the blog and rated it 5 Boundless stars.  When Isley approached us about reviewing the audiobook I decided to take it since Stormi doesn’t like audiobooks and I love them.<br/><br/>This story is reminiscent of the Gwyneth Paltrow movie Sliding doors.  There are two choices that happen and two different stories with the same character that take place in different timeline/dimension.  The stories are sweet, clean and sappy.  Much like a Julia Roberts romantic comedy, Runaway </span>
  <span id="freeText5883901602903885485" style="display:none">Stormi originally read this for the blog and rated it 5 Boundless stars.  When Isley approached us about reviewing the audiobook I decided to take it since Stormi doesn’t like audiobooks and I love them.<br /><br />This story is reminiscent of the Gwyneth Paltrow movie Sliding doors.  There are two choices that happen and two different stories with the same character that take place in different timeline/dimension.  The stories are sweet, clean and sappy.  Much like a Julia Roberts romantic comedy, Runaway Bride comes to mind.  The theme of the stories is to follow your heart.  <br /><br />I would have enjoyed this book more had I read it.  I listen to a lot of audiobooks; I typically am listening to one every day, so I am pretty picky about narrators.  A narrator will make or break the audiobook.  Cook’s narration of this story didn’t flow.  I could tell she was reading the story; she didn’t bring any life or zest to the characters.  Her narration fell flat for me, her pacing was off, and there was no deviation from one character to the next.  <br /><br />Overall I am giving this audiobook 3 Boundless stars.  The narrator would get less, and the book would get more.  </span>
  <a data-text-id="5883901602903885485" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2570833230" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1984816060350155781">This is the first book in the series, they can all be read as a standalone though. I found Camilla has a way that she manages to connect with her readers and her writing is really thought out. In this story we meet Gemma and the chapters switch from her going to her best mate and also her going to her ex. I loved getting to know the characters and look forward to the next instalment. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Al9v5hjUB0WQR6LFuoYbfZoXl/P+YbtftoV51pqJ+EsU7mit4cDMS5NCzmZwLwW0Pv/6ukfvpwa34A5kXVYV+w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EDTvuWF3A9ShzKC+Hk8tpEyBm9wtWavHm+gGOiIT7XEGhejymGPI2qLJzB3U5jNt6Gn2lZTXt56ajXGI5cwAwQ==')})
  }
